###Issue of Мелвис### II
150159 = {
	name="Прентис"	#Canon
	dynasty=159

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"

	father=16159
	mother=46159

	add_trait=underhanded_rogue
	add_trait=proud
	add_trait=ambitious	

	8020.1.1 = {birth="8020.1.1" }
	8036.1.1 = {add_trait=knight add_trait=poor_warrior}
	8043.1.1={ #Faith Militant Uprising
		add_spouse=450159
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8043.5.10 } }
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_vassal = { set_character_flag = supporting_king }
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	8048.3.1 = { #Rogar Baratheon Rebellion
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8048.3.7 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				any_vassal = { 
					set_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = against_king
				}
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
		}
	}	
	8059.2.1={
		add_trait="ill" 
		death = { death_reason = death_trait } # Died of Shivers
	}
}

###Issue of Эдмин### III
15159 = {
	name="Гровер"	# Grandfather of Эльмо. Great Grandfather of Кермит, lord During the Dance
	dynasty=159

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"

	father=150159
	mother=450159

	add_trait=tough_soldier
	add_trait=wroth
	add_trait=stubborn

	8049.1.1 = {
		birth="8049.1.1" 
		effect = {
			health = 4
		}
	}
	8065.1.1 = {add_trait=knight add_trait=poor_warrior}
	8068.1.1 = {add_spouse=60800149} #Bracken, as another possible reason why he supported greens
	8110.1.1 = { add_trait=blinded_age }
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		add_trait=incapable
		effect = {
			random_courtier = {
				limit = { character = 14159 }
				give_minor_title = title_regent
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.5.5 } }
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
				set_defacto_liege=THIS
				any_vassal = { 
					set_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = against_king
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_dithered
							who = ROOT
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.5.5 = {
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_dithered
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			any_vassal = {
				clr_character_flag = neutral
			}
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.6.5 = {death="8130.6.5"}
}

			c_dragonstone = {

					opinion = {

						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}

						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		death = {death_reason = death_trait}
	}

###Issue of Эльмо### VI
13159 = {
	name="Кермит"	# Медгар grandfather. Lord of Riverrun at the time of the Dornish Conquest.
	dynasty=159
	
	martial=7

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"
	
	add_trait="quick"
	add_trait="brave"
	add_trait="diligent"
	add_trait="authoritative"
	add_trait="skilled_tactician"

	father=14159 # Эльмо Tully
	mother=44159

	8112.1.1 = {birth="8112.1.1"  }
	8128.1.1 = {add_trait=knight add_trait=skilled_warrior} #Killed Borros Baratheon
	8130.7.14 = { #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {

		}

					limit = {

				}

						}

				}
				d_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = {

							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}

							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.5.5 } } #Lord Tully joined war on the same side
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
							ROOT = {
								join_attacker_wars = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8131.1.1={
		death= {
			death_reason = death_battle
			killer = 14317 #Borros Baratheon
		}
	}
}

5500137 = {
	name="Джонотор" # a Lord at the time of the Dance of Dragons. Married Эсмена Bracken
	dynasty=137
	
	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"
	
	father=108137 # Клеос Darry
	mother=4590137
	
	8101.1.1 = {birth="8101.1.1"}
	8117.1.1={ add_trait="knight" add_trait=trained_warrior add_spouse=88000405}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
			}
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.7.1 = {
		death= {
			death_reason = death_battle
			killer = 77014 #Aemond
		}
	}
}

570138 = {
	name="Манфрид" # Second son of Джонах Mooton
	dynasty=138
	
	religion="the_seven"
	culture="riverlander"
	
	father=19138 # Джонах Mooton
	mother=450138
	
	add_trait=honorable
	add_trait=diligent
	add_trait=kind
	
	8099.1.1 = {birth="8099.1.1"}
	8115.1.1 = {
		add_trait="knight"
		add_trait="trained_warrior"
	}
	8130.5.9 = {	#Switched sides to Aegon
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8134.5.8 = {
		add_trait = ill
		death="8134.5.8" #Died of age and illness
	} 
}

				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT

						who = ROOT
						years = 100

	8090.1.1 = {add_trait=naive_appeaser add_trait=knight add_trait=trained_warrior}
	8129.3.3={
		effect={
			e_iron_throne= {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { imprison = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8129.8.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.8.1 = {
		effect = {						#Switches sides to Aegon
			prisoner = no
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } #riverlands
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8132.1.1 = {death="8132.1.1"}
